In_IN Tando_NNP Allahyar_NNP Taluka_NNP ,_, the_DT Mukhtiarkar_NNP reported_VBD that_DT sufficient_JJ proof_NN could_MD not_RB be_VB had_VBN and_CC stated_VBN that_IN the_DT enquiry_NN made_VBN in_IN the_DT matter_NN which_WDT created_VBD a_DT deep_JJ impression_NN among_IN the_DT people_NNS ,_, will_MD serve_VB as_IN a_DT deterant_NN against_IN any_DT further_JJ recurrence_NN of_IN this_DT sort_NN ._.

A_DT Circular_NNP was_VBD issued_VBN to_TO all_PDT the_DT Collectors_NNPS and_CC Deputy_NNP Commis-_NNP sioner_NN ,_, Upper_NNP Sind_NNP Frontier_NNP ,_, informing_VBG them_PRP that_IN although_IN arm_NN to_TO arm_VB vaccination_NN had_VBD been_VBN abolished_VBN since_IN many_JJ years_NNS some_DT vacci-_JJ nators_NNS taking_VBG advantage_NN of_IN the_DT ignorance_NN of_IN the_DT village_NN people_NNS threaten_VBP to_TO use_VB their_PRP$ vaccinated_JJ children_NNS as_IN vaccinifers_NNS for_IN purpose_NN of_IN extorting_VBG money_NN ,_, and_CC requesting_VBG them_PRP to_TO ask_VB the_DT Revenue_NN Officials_NNP to_TO make_VB a_DT special_JJ effort_NN to_TO remove_VB the_DT ignorance_NN of_IN the_DT people_NNS in_IN this_DT respect_NN and_CC to_TO inform_VB them_PRP to_TO report_VB in_IN such_JJ cases_NNS to_TO the_DT Mukhtiarkar_NNP or_CC Collector_NNP ._.
